        						        						<h1 class="artist"><a href="artist/Red-Hot-Chili-Peppers/5241">Red Hot Chili Peppers</a></h1>
        					</div>
        					<p class="artist hidden-sm hidden-md hidden-lg"><a href="artist/Red-Hot-Chili-Peppers/5241">Red Hot Chili Peppers</a></p>
        												<p class="artist-bio">Red Hot Chili Peppers are an American rock band formed in Los Angeles in 1983. The group's musical style primarily consists of rock with an emphasis on funk, as well as elements from other genres such as punk rock and psychedelic rock. Live, they incorporate many aspects of jam rock due to the improvised nature of much of their performances. Currently, the band consists of founding members Anthony Kiedis (vocals) and Michael "Flea" Balzary (bass), longtime drummer Chad Smith, and guitarist Josh Klinghoffer, who joined in late 2009, following the departure of John Frusciante. The Red Hot Chili Peppers have won seven Grammy Awards and sold over 80 million albums worldwide. In 2012 they were inducted into the Rock and Roll Hall of Fame.</p>
							<p class="artist-bio-link">
								<a href="addbio.php?aid=5241">Update this biography &raquo;</a><br>

							</p>
